Here's the plan for the Option C fix:\n\n**The Problem:**\nWhen ED Board bridge patients are loaded via `loadEDAdmissions()`, the hardcoded EVENTS still fire at their scheduled times. So if a learner admitted a DKA from ED Board, they get that patient AND Marcus Webb (DKA) shows up at 11 PM. Same for NSTEMI and COPD if those are ever added to ED Board.\n\n**The Fix (Option C):**\nAfter loading ED bridge patients in `startShift()`, check which diagnoses overlap with NF built-in ED admissions. For matching diagnoses, replace the built-in NF event with the ED bridge patient's identity and history, but keep the same time slot and orders template. When there's no match, keep the built-in event as-is.\n\n\nI'm mapping the collision points between NF's hardcoded events and ED Board cases\u2014DKA and NSTEMI are the current matches, with COPD future-proofed\u2014then implementing the suppression logic in `startShift()` to swap out the built-in patient data while preserving the event timing and clinical workflow. or replace it with a \"bridge version\" that uses the ED patient's identity)\n3. For non-matches: keep the NF event as-is\n\nSince these ED patients are already on the census from the bridge, the NF event shouldn't create a duplicate. The cleanest approach is to scan the EVENTS array after loading ED admissions, check each `ed-call` type event against existing bridge patients with matching diagnoses, and either skip the event or replace it with a check-in call about that patient.\n\nI think the simplest solution is to define a mapping from NF event IDs to ED Board variant IDs, then in `startShift()` after loading ED admissions, filter or modify the EVENTS array to suppress or replace built-in ED admissions that collide with bridge patients.
